-- Name: archive(); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: archive; Owner: sennder

CREATE FUNCTION archive.archive() RETURNS trigger
    LANGUAGE plpgsql SECURITY DEFINER
    AS $_$
    DECLARE
        archive_table_name text;
        insert_stmt text;
        archive_row archive.archive;
    BEGIN
        IF (TG_WHEN <> 'AFTER' OR TG_LEVEL <> 'ROW') THEN
            RAISE EXCEPTION 'archive function is only supported for AFTER ROW triggers';
        ELSEIF TG_OP = 'DELETE' THEN
            -- Convert the old row into the archive format
            archive_row = ROW(
                nextval('archive.archive_id_seq'),  -- id
                clock_timestamp(),                  -- rev_timestamp
                'DELETE',                           -- row_op
                TG_TABLE_SCHEMA::text,              -- row_schema
                TG_TABLE_NAME::text,                -- row_table
                NULL,                               -- row_pkeys (we'll get them next)
                to_jsonb(OLD)                       -- row_values
            );
            -- Pull the primary key(s) values out of the row_values based on the pkeys provided to the trigger
            SELECT  jsonb_object_agg(x, archive_row.row_values->x)
            INTO archive_row.row_pkeys
            FROM unnest((TG_ARGV[0])::text[]) x;
        ELSE
            RAISE EXCEPTION 'archive function currently only supports DELETE triggers';
        END IF;
        -- Calculate the partition name
        archive_table_name := 'archive_' || replace(date_trunc('month',archive_row.rev_timestamp)::date::text, '-', '_');
        -- Build the insert statement including the partition name
        insert_stmt := format($SQL$ INSERT INTO archive.%s (
                                    id,
                                    rev_timestamp,
                                    row_op,
                                    row_schema,
                                    row_table,
                                    row_pkeys,
                                    row_values)
                                VALUES ( $1.* )
                        $SQL$, archive_table_name);
        BEGIN
            -- Assume partitions exists
            EXECUTE insert_stmt USING archive_row;
        EXCEPTION WHEN UNDEFINED_TABLE THEN
        -- Create a new partition for this month
            BEGIN
                EXECUTE format(
                    $SQL$
                        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS archive.%1$s PARTITION OF archive.archive (
                            PRIMARY KEY (id)
                        ) FOR VALUES FROM (%3$L) TO (%4$L);
                        CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS %2$s
                        ON archive.%1$s (rev_timestamp);
                    $SQL$,
                    archive_table_name,
                    archive_table_name || '_idx',
                    date_trunc('month',archive_row.rev_timestamp)::date::text,
                    date_trunc('month',(archive_row.rev_timestamp + INTERVAL '1 month'))::date::text
                );
            -- A concurrent transaction has created the new partition so do nothing
            EXCEPTION WHEN OTHERS THEN
                NULL;
            END;
            -- Now insert into the new partition
                EXECUTE insert_stmt USING archive_row;
            END;
            RETURN NULL;
        END;
$_$;


ALTER FUNCTION archive.archive() OWNER TO sennder;

-- TOC entry 1867 (class 1255 OID 5194778)
-- Name: set_created_modified(); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: sennder
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.set_created_modified() RETURNS trigger
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $$
                DECLARE
                    exec_ts TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT clock_timestamp();
                BEGIN
                    IF TG_WHEN <> 'BEFORE' THEN
                        RAISE EXCEPTION 'set_created_modified function is only supported for BEFORE triggers';
                    ELSIF TG_OP = 'INSERT' THEN
                        -- Set created & modified to the same value (currnt execution time)
                        NEW.created = exec_ts;
                        NEW.modified = exec_ts;
                        RETURN NEW;
                    ELSIF TG_OP = 'UPDATE' THEN
                        --Override potential 'created' changes & set modified timestamp to the current execution time
                        NEW.created = OLD.created;
                        NEW.modified = exec_ts;
                        RETURN NEW;
                    ELSE
                        RAISE EXCEPTION 'set_created_modified function is only supported for UPDATE OR INSERT triggers';
                    END IF;
                END;
            $$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.set_created_modified() OWNER TO sennder;

--
-- TOC entry 1869 (class 1255 OID 5196379)
-- Name: set_tenant(); Type: FUNCTION; Schema: public; Owner: sennder
--

CREATE FUNCTION public.set_tenant() RETURNS trigger
    LANGUAGE plpgsql
    AS $$
    BEGIN
        -- Assure that we are in a BEFORE trigger
        IF TG_WHEN <> 'BEFORE' THEN
            RAISE EXCEPTION 'set_tenant function is only supported for BEFORE triggers';
        -- If the operation was done by the master user then do not assign/override the tenant
        ELSIF current_user = 'sennder' THEN
            RETURN NEW;
        -- Otherwise if it is a new row then set the tenant to the user that executed the operation
        ELSIF TG_OP = 'INSERT' THEN
            NEW.tenant = current_user;
            RETURN NEW;
        -- If it is an update then prevent the tenant user from being changed
        ELSIF TG_OP = 'UPDATE' THEN
            NEW.tenant = OLD.tenant;
            RETURN NEW;
        -- Base case error assumes that the trigger has been defined wrongly
        ELSE
            RAISE EXCEPTION 'set_tenant function is only supported for UPDATE OR INSERT triggers';
        END IF;
END;
$$;


ALTER FUNCTION public.set_tenant() OWNER TO sennder;

    pickup_start timestamp with time zone,
    pickup_end timestamp with time zone,

    executed_timestamp timestamp with time zone,

    credit_note_was_sent boolean NOT NULL,
    pallet_carrier_company_id integer,

    diesel_floater_id integer,
